    def _load_and_remap_matrix(ckpt_path,
                               old_tensor_name,
                               new_row_vocab_offset,
                               num_rows_to_load,
                               new_col_vocab_size,
                               initializer,
                               old_row_vocab_size=-1,
                               old_row_vocab_file=None,
                               new_row_vocab_file=None,
                               old_col_vocab_file=None,
                               new_col_vocab_file=None,
                               num_row_oov_buckets=0,
                               num_col_oov_buckets=0,
                               max_rows_in_memory=-1): ...
    	initializer([
        num_rows_to_load * new_col_vocab_size -
        num_rows_present * num_cols_present, 1
    ])
    	initializer([num_row_oov_buckets, new_col_vocab_size])
    	initializer(
        [num_rows_to_load + num_row_oov_buckets, num_col_oov_buckets])

            zero_output_for_mask=False): ...

                                       tuple(states) + tuple(constants))
    	step_function(inp, tuple(states) + tuple(constants))
    	step_function(
        input_time_zero, tuple(initial_states) + tuple(constants))
    	step_function(current_input,
                                       tuple(states) + tuple(constants))
    	step_function(current_input,
                                       tuple(states) + tuple(constants))

    def while_loop(cond,
                   body,
                   loop_vars,
                   shape_invariants=None,
                   parallel_iterations=10,
                   back_prop=True,
                   swap_memory=False,
                   name=None,
                   maximum_iterations=None,

    def while_loop(cond,
                   body,
                   loop_vars,
                   shape_invariants=None,
                   parallel_iterations=10,
                   maximum_iterations=None,
                   name=None,
                   return_same_structure=True,
                   back_prop=True): ...
    	cond(*_pack_sequence_as(orig_loop_vars, args))
    	body(*_pack_sequence_as(orig_loop_vars, args))

    def while_loop(condition: Callable[..., Any],
                   body: Callable[..., Any],
                   inputs: Optional[List[Any]] = None,
                   infeed_queue: Optional[tpu_feed.InfeedQueue] = None,
                   name: Any = None) -> Any: ...
    	condition(*inputs)
    	body(*(inputs + dequeue_ops))

    def while_stmt(test,
                   body,
                   get_state,
                   set_state,
                   init_vars,
                   basic_symbol_names,
                   composite_symbol_names,
                   opts): ...
    	test(*init_vars)
    	body(*init_vars)

    def while_stmt(test, body, get_state, set_state, symbol_names, opts): ...
    	test()
    	body()

    def wrap(op, alpha, dtype, shape, seed): ...
    	op(seed=seed, shape=shape,
              alpha=constant_op.constant(alpha, dtype=dtype), dtype=dtype)

    def wrap(op, dtype, shape, shape_dtype, seed, **kwargs): ...
    	op(seed=seed, shape=shape_, dtype=dtype, **kwargs)

    def wrap(op, lam, lam_dtype, out_dtype, shape, seed): ...
    	op(seed=seed, shape=shape,
              lam=constant_op.constant(lam_dtype(lam), dtype=lam_dtype),
              dtype=out_dtype)
    	lam_dtype(lam)

    def wrap(op, logits, logits_dtype, output_dtype, seed): ...
    	op(seed=seed,
              logits=constant_op.constant(logits, dtype=logits_dtype),
              num_samples=num_samples, output_dtype=output_dtype)

    def wrap(op, minval, maxval, shape, shape_dtype, dtype, seed, **kwargs): ...
    	op(
        seed=seed, shape=shape_, minval=minval, maxval=maxval, dtype=dtype,
        **kwargs)

    def wrap_f(f): ...
    	f(self, *args, **kwargs)
    	f(self, *args, **kwargs)

    def wrap_py_func(f, return_dtypes, args, kwargs=None, use_dummy_return=False): ...
    	f(*f_args, **f_kwargs)

    def wrap_with_counts(self, method_name, method): ...
    	method(*args, **kwargs)

    def wrap_with_counts(self, method_name, method): ...
    	method(*args, **kwargs)

    def wrapped_method(method_to_wrap, name, *arg, **kwargs): ...
    	method_to_wrap(*arg, **kwargs)

    def wrapper_decorator(f): ...
    	f(*args, **kwargs)

    def wrapping_decorator(f): ...
    	f(*args, **kwargs)

    def write(tag, tensor, step=None, metadata=None, name=None): ...
    	tensor()

    def xla_allow_fallback_impl(func): ...
    	func(self, *args, **kwargs)
    	func(self, *args, **kwargs)
